gpt_setAolTargeting();
}
}
googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
gpt_request.renderedSlotCnt++;
if (gpt_request.renderedSlotCnt == 1) {
st_parseBidTargeting();
}
if (gpt_request.renderedSlotCnt == gpt_request.refreshSlotCnt) {
st_gptRenderCompletedCallback();
}
gpt_logAdLineItemId(event);
var lineItemId = event.lineItemId || "null";
// TODO cleaner way to create and manage object data
var slot = event.slot;
var slotIdx = slot.tpxSlotIdx;
var targeting = stats_parseSlotKeyTargeting(slot);
gpt_request.renderedSlotData[slotIdx] = new Object();
gpt_request.renderedSlotData[slotIdx].lineItemId = lineItemId;
gpt_request.renderedSlotData[slotIdx].targeting = targeting;
});
googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
if (gpt_request.technorati &amp;&amp; TN8 ) {
TN8.SmartWrapper.setTargeting(gptadslots);
}
else {
googletag.enableServices();
}
stars_sendLoadStat("ads-gptsetupdone");
});
}
if (!st_request.isIFrame) {
if (!gpt_request.yieldbot) {
st_setupGPTSlotsDesktop();
// Just has to be called after GPT is fully initialized
if (gpt_request.sonobi_loaded)
callSonobi();
if (st_request.useRealtimeQueue)
updateRealtimeTargeting();
}
else {
ybotq.push(st_setupGPTSlotsDesktop);
ybotq.push(callSonobi);
}
}
function gpt_insertGlamPositions() {
for(var ii = 0; ii &lt; gpt_glamPositions.length; ii++) {
var div = $("#div-gpt-ad-" + gpt_glamPositions[ii].slotIdx);
if (st_request.inside) {
console.log('inserting ' + gpt_glamPositions[ii].id + ' into ' + div.attr("id"));
}
div.html('&lt;scri' + 'pt type="text/javascript"&gt;GlamShowIframeSlot("' + gpt_glamPositions[ii].id + '", "' + div.attr("id") + '")&lt;/s' + 'cript&gt;');
}
}
function gpt_updateSlideKeyvalue(newValue) {
googletag.pubads().setTargeting('slide', newValue);
}
// Interstitial that appears in place of a Slide image
function loadInterstitialAd() {
$('.js-int-ad-wrapper').html("&lt;div id='div-gpt-ad-4' class='x-ad js-gpt-hide'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");
$('.js-int-ad-wrapper').show();
if (bInterstitialLoaded) {
if (st_request.inside)
console.log('refresh interstitial');
if (gptadslots[4])
if (gpt_request.technorati) {
if (st_request.staging) {
console.log("WARNING!!! interstitial not tested with technorati on new stars-slidehow.tt because it was partially disabled");
}
TN8.SmartWrapper.setTargeting([gptadslots[4]]);
}
else {
googletag.pubads().refresh([gptadslots[4]]);
}
}
else {
if (st_request.inside)
console.log('load interstitial');
googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-4'); });
}
}
function hideInterstitialAd() {
if (st_request.inside)
console.log('hide interstitial');
$('.js-int-ad-wrapper').hide();
$('.js-int-ad-wrapper').html("");
}
function slide_isGlamInterval() {
return ((st_request.slideNum) % st_request.fullPageRefreshInterval == 0);
}
function st_refreshAds() {
try {
st_refreshAdsInternal();
}
catch (e) {
stars_sendExceptionStat("slide-refreshAds", e);
}
}
function st_refreshAdsInternal() {
if (!st_request.adRefresh)
return false;
var now = (new Date()).getTime();
if (false) {
if ((now - lastAdRefresh) &lt; 4000) {
if (st_request.inside)
console.log('ad throttle');
return false;
}
}
if (st_request.inside)
console.log('ad refresh');
lastAdRefresh = now;
if (gpt_request.glam &amp;&amp; gpt_request.glam_advanced &amp;&amp; slide_isGlamInterval()) {
gpt_insertGlamPositions();
return false;
}
if (st_request.showRealtimeAds) {
reloadRealtimeAdBids();
}
var slotArr = $.grep(gpt_request.gpt_adslots, function(obj, idx) {
return obj &amp;&amp; !obj.interslide &amp;&amp; obj.tpxSlotIdx != 0;
});
if (st_request.noRefresh728x90TopAd) {
slotArr = $.grep(slotArr, function(obj, idx) {
return (obj.topAd == 1 ? false : true);
});
}
if (st_request.noRefresh300x250Ad) {
slotArr = $.grep(slotArr, function(obj, idx) {
return (obj.rectAd == 1 ? false : true);
});
}
if (st_request.noRefresh300x600Ad) {
slotArr = $.grep(slotArr, function(obj, idx) {
return (obj.tallRectAd == 1 ? false : true);
});
}
if (st_request.noRefresh728x90BottomAd) {
slotArr = $.grep(slotArr, function(obj, idx) {
return (obj.botAd == 1 ? false : true);
});
}
if (st_request.delayTopAdRefresh) {
var currentTime = (new Date()).getTime();
var refreshTopAd = true;
if (!st_request.topAdLoaded) {
refreshTopAd = false;
stars_sendBackfillStat("topadtest-skip-notloaded");
}
else if (currentTime - st_request.topAdLoaded &lt; 2000) {
refreshTopAd = false;
stars_sendBackfillStat("topadtest-skip-2000");
}
if (!refreshTopAd) {
slotArr = $.grep(slotArr, function(obj, idx) {
return !obj.topAd;
});
}
}
gpt_request.refreshSlotCnt = slotArr.length;
gpt_request.renderedSlotCnt = 0;
if (gpt_request.technorati) {
TN8.SmartWrapper.setTargeting(slotArr);
}
else {
googletag.pubads().refresh(slotArr);
}
return false;
}
  </script>
  <!-- End: GPT -->

}
else {
clickableDivs.outerWidth(divWidth).removeClass('x-hidden');
}
}

//Set the URL to be clicked.

          <a class="x-pinterest btn-social-share js-pinterest" data-eventlabel="multishare" data-social-type="pinterest-share" href="#">
           <span class="ico-pinterest-circle">
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="str-overlay-subcaption js-overlay-caption">
          <div class="x-subcaption-wrapper js-subcaption-wrapper">
           <p class="x-slide-subcaption js-slide-subcaption">
            The double-amputee olympic runner received a 5-year jail sentence for killing his girlfriend Reeva Steencamp by shooting at her through their bathroom door during an argument.
           </p>

         <h2 class="js-slide-caption x-slide-caption">
          Dog the Bounty Hunter
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="str-slideshow js-slideshow">
         <div class="str-multi-share">

         <h2 class="js-slide-caption x-slide-caption">
          Ted Kennedy
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="str-slideshow js-slideshow">
         <div class="str-multi-share">
          <a class="x-fb btn-social-share js-social-share" data-eventlabel="multishare" data-social-type="fb-share" href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http%3A//stars%2Etopix%2Ecom/slideshow/14852">
           <span class="ico-facebook">
           </span>
          </a>
          <a class="x-twitter btn-social-share js-social-share" data-eventlabel="multishare" data-social-type="twitter-share" href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=37%20Celebrities%20Who%20Killed%20Someone%20In%20Real%20Life&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fstars.topix.com%2Fslideshow%2F14852&amp;via=TopixStars">
           <span class="ico-twitter">
           </span>
          </a>
          <a class="x-pinterest btn-social-share js-pinterest" data-eventlabel="multishare" data-social-type="pinterest-share" href="#">
           <span class="ico-pinterest-circle">
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="str-overlay-subcaption js-overlay-caption">
          <div class="x-subcaption-wrapper js-subcaption-wrapper">
           <p class="x-slide-subcaption js-slide-subcaption">
            In 1969, after drinking at a party, Ted Kennedy drove his car off a bridge in Chappaquiddick. His passenger Mary Jo Kopechne drowned in the vehicle. Kennedy fled the scene and didn't report the accident for 9 hours, for which he received a 2-month suspended sentence.
           </p>
          </div>

          <a class="x-twitter btn-social-share js-social-share" data-eventlabel="multishare" data-social-type="twitter-share" href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=37%20Celebrities%20Who%20Killed%20Someone%20In%20Real%20Life&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fstars.topix.com%2Fslideshow%2F14852&amp;via=TopixStars">
           <span class="ico-twitter">
           </span>
          </a>
          <a class="x-pinterest btn-social-share js-pinterest" data-eventlabel="multishare" data-social-type="pinterest-share" href="#">
           <span class="ico-pinterest-circle">
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="str-overlay-subcaption js-overlay-caption">
          <div class="x-subcaption-wrapper js-subcaption-wrapper">
           <p class="x-slide-subcaption js-slide-subcaption">
            NASCAR driver Tony Stewart hit and killed another driver, 20 year-old Kevin Ward. The two drivers had a minor collision on the track. Then when Ward exited his car, Stewart drove back around the track and struck Ward with his car. Stewart was later cleared of any wrongdoing.
           </p>

            The
            <i>
             Mork and Mindy
            </i>
            comic actress was charged with murdering her husband after she allegedly stabbed him to death with a letter opener in 1965.

});

stars_sendEvent('social', 'un-like', html_element.dataset.like);
});
});
$(document).ready(function() {
$(document).trigger('afterSlideChange');
$('.js-pinterest').on('click', function(elem) {
elem.preventDefault();
setPinterestHref();
social_shareClick($(this));
return true;
});
$('.js-social-share').on('click', function(elem) {
elem.preventDefault();
social_shareClick($(this));
return true;
});
$('.js-close-overlay').on('click', function() {
$(this).closest('.js-overlay-caption').toggleClass('x-closed').end()
.toggleClass('ico-arrow-up2 ico-arrow-down2').end()
.closest('.js-active').find('.js-prev-symbol, .js-next-symbol').toggleClass('x-darker-arrow-button');
stars_sendEvent("misc", "overlay-btn-click");
});
$(".js-prev").on('click', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
slide_prevSlide();
return false;
});
$(".js-next").on('click', function(e){
e.preventDefault();
slide_wrapperAdvance();
return false;
});
$(document).on('keydown', function(e) {
//37 is the keycode for the left arrow, 39 is the keycode for the right arrow
if (e.keyCode == 37) {
slide_wrapperPrev();
}
else if (e.keyCode == 39) {
slide_wrapperAdvance();
}
return true;
});
$('.js-vote-click').on('click', function(){
var selected = $(this);
var activeSlide = selected.closest('.js-active');
var photoId = activeSlide.find('.js-slide-img').attr('data-photoid');
var itemId = st_request.itemid;
var vote = $(this).attr('data-vote');
if (!selected.hasClass("x-selected") &amp;&amp; !selected.siblings().hasClass("x-selected")) {
stars_sendEvent('misc', 'vote-up', vote);
}
if (!selected.hasClass("x-selected")) {
st_slideVote(itemId, photoId, vote,
//Callback function to update textbox(es) count
function() {
var sameImage = $("img[data-photoid='" + photoId + "']");
sameImage.closest('.js-slide-item').each(function() {
var selectedButton = $(this).find(".js-vote-click[data-vote='"+ vote +"']");
var buttonParent = selectedButton.closest('.js-votes');
var buttons = buttonParent.find('.js-vote-click');
//If the user has already voted we decrement their original vote count
var originalVote = buttonParent.find('.x-selected').find('.js-vote-count');
if (originalVote.length) {
if (parseInt(originalVote.text()) &gt; 0) {
var countToDecrease = parseInt(originalVote.text());
originalVote.text(countToDecrease - 1);
}
}
//Update the selected button count
var voteCountContainer = selectedButton.find('.js-vote-count');
var countToIncrease = parseInt(voteCountContainer.text());
voteCountContainer.text(countToIncrease + 1);
buttons.removeClass('x-selected');
selectedButton.addClass('x-selected');
});
});
}
});
});
function loadImagesAfterSlideChange() {
var currentSlide = $('.js-active');
loadSlideImage(currentSlide, function() {
currentSlide.nextAll().slice(0, 2).each(function() {
loadSlideImage(this);
});
});
setTimeout(function() {
var currentImage = currentSlide.find('.js-slide-img');
if (currentImage.length &gt; 0) {
var imgelem = currentImage[0];
if (imgelem &amp;&amp; typeof(imgelem.naturalHeight) != "undefined") {
if (imgelem.naturalHeight &lt; 100) {
stars_sendExceptionStat("image-notloaded", currentImage.attr("src"));
stars_appendToTrackerLog("exception", "image-notLoaded " + (imgelem.complete ? "complete" : "not-complete") + " " + imgelem.naturalHeight + " " + currentImage.attr("src"));
}
}
}
}, 5000);
}
function loadSlideImage(slide, callback) {
var currentImage = $(slide).find('.js-slide-img');
var currentSlideImgUrl = currentImage.data('img-src');
currentImage.attr('src', currentSlideImgUrl);
if (callback) {
if (currentImage[0].complete) {
callback();
}
else {
currentImage.one('load', function () {
callback();
});
}
}
}
function slide_wrapperAdvance() {
try {
slide_advance();
}
catch (ex) {
stars_sendExceptionStat("slide-wrapperAdvance", ex);
}
return false;
}
function slide_wrapperPrev() {
try {
slide_prevSlide();
}
catch (ex) {
stars_sendExceptionStat("slide-wrapperPrevious", ex);
}
return false;
}
function slide_advance() {
var activeSlide = $('.js-active');
// If we are on the cover photo, hide it and show the regular slide
if (activeSlide.hasClass('js-cover')) {
// Prevent the cover from showing afterwards
st_request.onCover = 0;
slide_updateSlide(1);
return;
}
// Check for the last slide
if (activeSlide.next().length === 0) {
return slide_nextSlideShow();
}
if (st_request.fullPageRefresh) {
if (slide_isRefreshInterval()) {
return slide_refreshPageForNextSlide();
}
}
// Else increment slide index and update slide
st_request.slideNum++;
slide_updateSlide(1);
return false;
}
function slide_updateGPTSlideKV(val) {
try {
gpt_updateSlideKeyvalue(val);
}
catch (e) {
stars_sendExceptionStat("slide-updateGPTSlideKV", e);
}
}
function slide_isRefreshInterval() {
return ((st_request.slideNum + 1) % st_request.fullPageRefreshInterval == 0);
}
function slide_refreshPageForNextSlide() {
var baseSlideUrl = "/slideshow/14852/slide1";
var nextSlideNum = st_request.slideNum + 1;
var nextSlideNumStr = "slide" + nextSlideNum;
baseSlideUrl = baseSlideUrl.replace(/slide1/, nextSlideNumStr);
window.location = baseSlideUrl;
return false;
}
function slide_nextSlideShow() {
var nextUrl = '/next/' + st_request.itemid + '?no_cover=1';
window.location = nextUrl;
return false;
}
function slide_updateSlide(direction) {
var $activeSlide = $('.js-active');
$activeSlide.removeClass('js-active x-active');
if (direction &gt; 0) {
$activeSlide = $activeSlide.next('.js-slide-item');
}
else if (direction &lt; 0) {
$activeSlide = $activeSlide.prev('.js-slide-item');
}
$activeSlide.addClass('js-active x-active');
$(document).trigger('afterSlideChange');
//For netseer ad
repositionSlideAd();
stars_sendPageview(formatNum1000(st_request.slideNum));
slide_updateGPTSlideKV(formatNum1000(st_request.slideNum)); // must be before refreshAds()
st_refreshAds();
if (history &amp;&amp; history.pushState) {
// TODO use push state
// history.pushState({ slideNum: st_request.slideNum }, '', '/slideshow/' + st_request.itemid + '/slide' + st_request.slideNum);
}
return false;
}
function positionOverlayText(){
var activeSlide = $('.js-active');
if (activeSlide.hasClass('x-overlay')) {
var subcapWrapper = activeSlide.find('.js-subcaption-wrapper');
var subcapWrapperHeight = subcapWrapper.outerHeight();
var subcap = activeSlide.find('.js-slide-subcaption');
var subcapHeight = subcap.outerHeight();
var margin = parseInt((subcapWrapperHeight - subcapHeight) / 2);
var padding = 0;
if (margin &lt; 20) {
subcap.css({'padding-top': 30})
}
subcap.css({ 'margin-top': margin });
subcapWrapper.css('visibility','visible').hide().fadeIn(700);
}
}
function slide_prevSlide() {
var activeSlide = $('.js-active');
if (activeSlide.prev().length == 0 || activeSlide.prev().hasClass('js-cover')) {
return false;
}
st_request.slideNum--;
slide_updateSlide(-1);
return false;
}
function repositionSlideAd() {
$(window).scrollTop($(window).scrollTop() + 1);
$(window).scrollTop($(window).scrollTop() - 1);
}

       $('.js-star-rating').on('click', 'span', function () {
var self = $(this);
var parentContainer = self.closest('.js-star-rating');
var rating = self.attr('data-rating');
//set inputs value to selected rating
parentContainer.find('input').val(rating);
//Color the stars that have been selected
var allRatings = parentContainer.find('span');
//First remove all the ones that have been selected
allRatings.removeClass('x-rated');
//For each one, add the colored class
for(i = 0; i &lt; rating; i++) {
$(allRatings[i]).addClass('x-rated');
}
});

   <script>
    $(function() {
var tooltipContainer = $("#js-tooltip-container");
$(document).on('mouseover', '.js-tooltip', function(e) {
var tip = $(this).attr('data-tooltip');
tooltipContainer.html(tip).stop(true,true).fadeIn();
});
$(document).on('mousemove', '.js-tooltip', function(e) {
var tooltipWidth = tooltipContainer.outerWidth();
var tooltipHeight = tooltipContainer.outerHeight();
var pageWidth = $('body').width();
var pageHeight = $('body').height();
if (e.pageX &gt; pageWidth / 2) {
tooltipContainer.css('left', (e.pageX - tooltipWidth + 10) + "px");
}
else {
tooltipContainer.css('left', (e.pageX - 10) + "px");
}
if (e.pageY &gt; 100) {
tooltipContainer.css('top', (e.pageY - (tooltipHeight + 10)) + "px")
}
else {
tooltipContainer.css('top', (e.pageY + 10) + "px");
}
});
$(document).on('mouseout', ' .js-tooltip',
function(e) {
tooltipContainer.stop(true,true).fadeOut();
});
}());
   </script>

})();
window._fbq = window._fbq || [];
window._fbq.push(['track', 'PixelInitialized', {}]);
window._fbq.push(['track', 'VName', { name: st_request.vname }]);
window._fbq.push(['track', 'SessionCount', { count: st_request.sessionCount }]);
window._fbq.push(['track', '6025412190712', {'value':'0.00','currency':'USD'}]);
if (st_request.sessionCount &gt; 30) {
window._fbq.push(['track', "SessionOver30", {}]);
}
if (st_request.utm_source) {
window._fbq.push(['track', 'UtmSource', { source: st_request.utm_source }]);
}
if (isAmazonBid()) {
window._fbq.push(['track', "AmazonBid", {}]);
}
if (isCasaleBid()) {
window._fbq.push(['track', "CasaleBid", {}]);
}
if (isCriteoBid()) {
window._fbq.push(['track', "CriteoBid", {}]);
}
if (isSonobiBid()) {
window._fbq.push(['track', "SonobiBid", {}]);
}

window._fbq.push(['track', "AdBlockUser", {}]);
if (st_request.inside) {
console.log("AdBlockUser FB custom audience");
}
});
